einbroch.gat,246,70,0	script	Vote Timer#ein	139,{

OnInit:
	initnpctimer;
	end;

OnCommandOn:
	initnpctimer;
	end;

OnCommandOff1:
	donpcevent "Vote Timer2#ein::OnCommandOn";
	end;

OnCommandOff2:
	donpcevent "Vote Timer3#ein::OnCommandOn";
	end;

OnCommandOff3:
	donpcevent "Vote Timer4#ein::OnCommandOn";
	end;

OnTimer60000:
	set '@result,$050530_minus1_tupyo4;
	if ('@result == 1) {
		set '@kafra_point,$050530_minus1_tupyo6;
		set '@jonda_point,$050530_minus1_tupyo7;
		if ('@jonda_point == 0) {
			donpcevent "Vote Timer2#ein::OnCommandOn";
			stopnpctimer;
			end;
		} else if ('@jonda_point == 1) {
			if ('@kafra_point < 2) {
				donpcevent "Vote Timer2#ein::OnCommandOn";
				stopnpctimer;
				end;
			} else {
				donpcevent "Vote Timer3#ein::OnCommandOn";
				stopnpctimer;
				end;
			}
		} else {
			if ('@kafra_point < 2) {
				donpcevent "Vote Timer2#ein::OnCommandOn";
				stopnpctimer;
				end;
			} else {
				donpcevent "Vote Timer3#ein::OnCommandOn";
				stopnpctimer;
				end;
			}
		}
	} else if ('@result == 2) {
		set '@kafra_point,$050530_minus1_tupyo6;
		set '@jonda_point,$050530_minus1_tupyo7;
		if ('@jonda_point == 0) {
			donpcevent "Vote Timer2#ein::OnCommandOn";
			stopnpctimer;
			end;
		} else if ('@jonda_point == 1) {
			if ('@kafra_point < 2) {
				donpcevent "Vote Timer2#ein::OnCommandOn";
				stopnpctimer;
				end;
			} else {
				donpcevent "Vote Timer4#ein::OnCommandOn";
				stopnpctimer;
				end;
			}
		} else {
			if ('@kafra_point < 2) {
				donpcevent "Vote Timer2#ein::OnCommandOn";
				stopnpctimer;
				end;
			} else {
				donpcevent "Vote Timer4#ein::OnCommandOn";
				stopnpctimer;
				end;
			}
		}
	} else {
		set '@time,$050530_minus1_tupyo1;
		if ('@time == 1440) {
			set '@jonda,$050530_minus1_tupyo2;
			set '@kafra,$050530_minus1_tupyo3;
			if (('@jonda >= 20) || ('@kafra >= 20)) {
				set '@kafra_point,$050530_minus1_tupyo6;
				set '@jonda_point,$050530_minus1_tupyo7;
				if ('@jonda > '@kafra) {
					if ('@jonda_point == 0) {
						if ('@kafra_point < 2) {
							set '@kafra_point,'@kafra_point + 1;
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo6,'@kafra_point;
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo4,1;
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo1,0;
							donpcevent "ScrutinyAssociation#tim6::OnCommandOn";
							donpcevent "Vote Timer2#ein::OnCommandOn";
							end;
						} else if ('@kafra_point == 2) {
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo4,1;
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo1,0;
							donpcevent "ScrutinyAssociation#tim6::OnCommandOn";
							donpcevent "Vote Timer2#ein::OnCommandOn";
							end;
						}
					} else if ('@jonda_point == 1) {
						if ('@kafra_point < 2) {
							set '@kafra_point,'@kafra_point + 1;
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo6,'@kafra_point;
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo4,1;
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo1,0;
							donpcevent "ScrutinyAssociation#tim6::OnCommandOn";
							donpcevent "Vote Timer2#ein::OnCommandOn";
							end;
						} else {
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo1,0;
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo4,1;
							donpcevent "ScrutinyAssociation#tim6::OnCommandOn";
							donpcevent "Vote Timer3#ein::OnCommandOn";
							end;
						}
					} else {
						if ('@kafra_point < 2) {
							set '@kafra_point,'@kafra_point + 1;
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo6,'@kafra_point;
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo4,1;
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo1,0;
							donpcevent "ScrutinyAssociation#tim6::OnCommandOn";
							donpcevent "Vote Timer2#ein::OnCommandOn";
							end;
						} else {
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo4,1;
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo1,0;
							donpcevent "ScrutinyAssociation#tim6::OnCommandOn";
							donpcevent "Vote Timer3#ein::OnCommandOn";
							end;
						}
					}
				} else {
					if ('@kafra_point == 0) {
						if ('@jonda_point < 2) {
							set '@jonda_point,'@jonda_point + 1;
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo7,'@jonda_point;
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo4,2;
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo1,0;
							donpcevent "ScrutinyAssociation#tim7::OnCommandOn";
							donpcevent "Vote Timer2#ein::OnCommandOn";
							end;
						} else {
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo4,2;
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo1,0;
							donpcevent "ScrutinyAssociation#tim7::OnCommandOn";
							donpcevent "Vote Timer2#ein::OnCommandOn";
							end;
						}
					} else if ('@kafra_point == 1) {
						if ('@jonda_point < 2) {
							set '@jonda_point,'@jonda_point + 1;
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo7,'@jonda_point;
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo4,2;
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo1,0;
							donpcevent "ScrutinyAssociation#tim7::OnCommandOn";
							donpcevent "Vote Timer2#ein::OnCommandOn";
							end;
						} else {
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo4,2;
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo1,0;
							donpcevent "ScrutinyAssociation#tim7::OnCommandOn";
							donpcevent "Vote Timer4#ein::OnCommandOn";
							end;
						}
					} else {
						if ('@jonda_point < 2) {
							set '@jonda_point,'@jonda_point + 1;
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo7,'@jonda_point;
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo4,2;
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo1,0;
							donpcevent "ScrutinyAssociation#tim7::OnCommandOn";
							donpcevent "Vote Timer2#ein::OnCommandOn";
							end;
						} else {
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo4,2;
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo1,0;
							donpcevent "ScrutinyAssociation#tim7::OnCommandOn";
							donpcevent "Vote Timer4#ein::OnCommandOn";
							end;
						}
					}
				}
			} else {
				set $050530_minus1_tupyo4,3;
				set $050530_minus1_tupyo1,0;
				donpcevent "Vote Timer#ein::OnCommandOn";
				end;
			}
		} else {
			set '@time,'@time + 1;
			set $050530_minus1_tupyo1,'@time;
			donpcevent "Vote Timer#ein::OnCommandOn";
			end;
		}
	}
}

einbroch.gat,245,71,0	script	Vote Timer2#ein	139,{

OnCommandOn:
	initnpctimer;
	end;

OnTimer60000:
	set '@time2,$050530_minus1_tupyo5;
	if ('@time2 == 8640) {
		set $050530_minus1_tupyo5,0;
		set $050530_minus1_tupyo4,0;
		set $050530_minus1_tupyo3,0;
		set $050530_minus1_tupyo2,0;
		set '@check,$050530_minus1_tupyo8;
		set '@check,'@check + 1;
		set $050530_minus1_tupyo8,'@check;
		donpcevent "Vote Timer#ein::OnCommandOn";
		end;
	} else {
		set '@time2,'@time2 + 1;
		set $050530_minus1_tupyo5,'@time2;
		donpcevent "Vote Timer2#ein::OnCommandOn";
		end;
	}
}

einbroch.gat,246,71,0	script	Vote Timer3#ein	139,{

OnCommandOn:
	initnpctimer;
	end;

OnTimer60000:
	set '@time2,$050530_minus1_tupyo5;
	if ('@time2 == 8640) {
		set $050530_minus1_tupyo5,0;
		set $050530_minus1_tupyo4,0;
		set $050530_minus1_tupyo3,0;
		set $050530_minus1_tupyo2,0;
		set '@jonda_point,$050530_minus1_tupyo7;
		set '@jonda_point,'@jonda_point - 1;
		set $050530_minus1_tupyo7,'@jonda_point;
		set '@check,$050530_minus1_tupyo8;
		set '@check,'@check + 1;
		set $050530_minus1_tupyo8,'@check;
		donpcevent "Vote Timer#ein::OnCommandOn";
		end;
	} else {
		set '@time2,'@time2 + 1;
		set $050530_minus1_tupyo5,'@time2;
		donpcevent "Vote Timer3#ein::OnCommandOn";
		end;
	}
}

einbroch.gat,247,71,0	script	Vote Timer4#ein	139,{

OnCommandOn:
	initnpctimer;
	end;

OnTimer60000:
	set '@time2,$050530_minus1_tupyo5;
	if ('@time2 == 8640) {
		set $050530_minus1_tupyo5,0;
		set $050530_minus1_tupyo4,0;
		set $050530_minus1_tupyo3,0;
		set $050530_minus1_tupyo2,0;
		set '@kafra_point,$050530_minus1_tupyo6;
		set '@kafra_point,'@kafra_point - 1;
		set $050530_minus1_tupyo6,'@kafra_point;
		set '@check,$050530_minus1_tupyo8;
		set '@check,'@check + 1;
		set $050530_minus1_tupyo8,'@check;
		donpcevent "Vote Timer#ein::OnCommandOn";
		end;
	} else {
		set '@time2,'@time2 + 1;
		set $050530_minus1_tupyo5,'@time2;
		donpcevent "Vote Timer4#ein::OnCommandOn";
		end;
	}
}

yuno.gat,162,191,4	script	Kafra Voting Staff#yuno	861,{

	cutin "kafra_09",2;
	mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
	mes "Greetings, adventurer.";
	mes "As you may be aware, we";
	mes "are holding an election to";
	mes "determine which company will";
	mes "provide the Dungeon Teleport";
	mes "Service. How may I help you?";
	next;
	switch(select("Reason for Election","Cast a Vote","Use Teleport Service","Cancel")) {
	case 1:
		mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
		mes "Cool Event Corp and the";
		mes "Kafra Corporation have both";
		mes "been planning to provide a";
		mes "Teleport Service to dungeons.";
		next;
		mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
		mes "But due to technological";
		mes "limitations, only one company";
		mes "can serve as provider for this";
		mes "Dungeon Teleport Service at a";
		mes "time. There, both companies have agreed to hold special elections.";
		next;
		mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
		mes "Each company has its own";
		mes "policies and guarantees in";
		mes "regards to the Dungeon Teleport Service, and in this election, the";
		mes "customers will ultimately decide and choose what's best for them.";
		next;
		mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
		mes "For now, the Dungeon";
		mes "Teleport Service will be";
		mes "provided in a series of trial periods. This way, customers can";
		mes "see the benefits of both companies before making the final decision.";
		next;
		mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
		mes "If you are qualified,";
		mes "please vote in each election";
		mes "to decide which company will";
		mes "provide the Dungeon Teleport";
		mes "Service for the next trial period. Thank you for your support~";
		close2;
		cutin "kafra_09",255;
		end;
	case 2:
		if (lght_boss < 17) {
			mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
			mes "Oh, I'm so sorry, but you";
			mes "are currently not qualified to";
			mes "vote. For voting qualification";
			mes "information, please visit the";
			mes "Al De Baran Kafra Headquarters.";
			mes "Thank you and have a nice day.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_09",255;
			end;
		} else {
			set '@result,$050530_minus1_tupyo4;
			if ('@result == 0) {
				set '@check,$050530_minus1_tupyo8;
				if (lght_tupyo <= '@check) {
					set '@kafra_point,$050530_minus1_tupyo6;
					if ('@kafra_point == 0) {
						mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
						mes "We, the Kafra Corporation,";
						mes "are planning to provide the";
						mes "Dungeon Teleport Service";
						mes "to the following dungeons...";
						next;
						mes "";
						mes "";
						mes "^FF0000Toy Factory, Level 2^000000";
						next;
						mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
						mes "If you are interested in";
						mes "a Teleport Service to this";
						mes "area, then please vote for";
						mes "us. Would you like to vote";
						mes "for the Kafra Corporation?";
						next;
						switch(select("No","Yes")) {
						case 1:
							mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
							mes "I understand. But if you";
							mes "happen to change your mind,";
							mes "you are welcome to come back";
							mes "at any time. Thank you and";
							mes "have a good day, adventurer.";
							close2;
							cutin "kafra_09",255;
							end;
						case 2:
							set '@check,$050530_minus1_tupyo8;
							set '@check,'@check + 1;
							set lght_tupyo,'@check;
							set '@kafra,$050530_minus1_tupyo3;
							set '@kafra,'@kafra + 1;
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo3,'@kafra;
							mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
							mes "Thanks for your vote!";
							mes "We'll continue to do our best";
							mes "to provide the highest quality";
							mes "service to our customers. Have";
							mes "a good day and remember that the Kafra service is on your side~";
							close2;
							cutin "kafra_09",255;
							end;
						}
					} else if ('@kafra_point == 1) {
						mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
						mes "We, the Kafra Corporation,";
						mes "are planning to provide the";
						mes "Dungeon Teleport Service";
						mes "to the following dungeons...";
						next;
						mes "";
						mes "";
						mes "^FF0000Toy Factory, Level 2^000000";
						mes "^FF0000Al De Baran Clock Tower, Level 3 ^000000";
						next;
						mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
						mes "If you are interested in";
						mes "a Teleport Service to these";
						mes "areas, then please vote for";
						mes "us. Would you like to vote";
						mes "for the Kafra Corporation?";
						next;
						switch(select("No","Yes")) {
						case 1:
							mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
							mes "I understand. But if you";
							mes "happen to change your mind,";
							mes "you are welcome to come back";
							mes "at any time. Thank you and";
							mes "have a good day, adventurer.";
							close2;
							cutin "kafra_09",255;
							end;
						case 2:
							set '@check,$050530_minus1_tupyo8;
							set '@check,'@check + 1;
							set lght_tupyo,'@check;
							set '@kafra,$050530_minus1_tupyo3;
							set '@kafra,'@kafra + 1;
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo3,'@kafra;
							mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
							mes "Thanks for your vote!";
							mes "We'll continue to do our best";
							mes "to provide the highest quality";
							mes "service to our customers. Have";
							mes "a good day and remember that the Kafra service is on your side~";
							close2;
							cutin "kafra_09",255;
							end;
						}
					} else {
						mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
						mes "We, the Kafra Corporation,";
						mes "are planning to provide the";
						mes "Dungeon Teleport Service";
						mes "to the following dungeons...";
						next;
						mes "";
						mes "";
						mes "^FF0000Toy Factory, Level 2^000000";
						mes "^FF0000Al De Baran Clock Tower, Level 3 Lava Dungeon, Level 2^000000";
						next;
						mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
						mes "If you are interested in";
						mes "a Teleport Service to these";
						mes "areas, then please vote for";
						mes "us. Would you like to vote";
						mes "for the Kafra Corporation?";
						next;
						switch(select("No","Yes")) {
						case 1:
							mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
							mes "I understand. But if you";
							mes "happen to change your mind,";
							mes "you are welcome to come back";
							mes "at any time. Thank you and";
							mes "have a good day, adventurer.";
							close2;
							cutin "kafra_09",255;
							end;
						case 2:
							set '@check,$050530_minus1_tupyo8;
							set '@check,'@check + 1;
							set lght_tupyo,'@check;
							set '@kafra,$050530_minus1_tupyo3;
							set '@kafra,'@kafra + 1;
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo3,'@kafra;
							mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
							mes "Thanks for your vote!";
							mes "We'll continue to do our best";
							mes "to provide the highest quality";
							mes "service to our customers. Have";
							mes "a good day and remember that the Kafra service is on your side~";
							close2;
							cutin "kafra_09",255;
							end;
						}
					}
				} else {
					mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
					mes "I'm sorry, but you've";
					mes "already participated in";
					mes "this election. When the next";
					mes "election comes, you will be";
					mes "able to vote once again.";
					mes "Thank you for your support~";
					close2;
					cutin "kafra_09",255;
					end;
				}
			} else if ('@result == 3) {
				set '@check,$050530_minus1_tupyo8;
				if (lght_tupyo <= '@check) {
					set '@kafra_point,$050530_minus1_tupyo6;
					if ('@kafra_point == 0) {
						mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
						mes "After totalling the number of";
						mes "votes from the last election,";
						mes "we have concluded that the";
						mes "minimum voter participation";
						mes "condition was not satisfied.";
						next;
						mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
						mes "Therefore, another election to";
						mes "determine which company will";
						mes "provide the Dungeon Teleport";
						mes "Service will be held. The Kafra";
						mes "Corporation will teleport to";
						mes "the following dungeons...";
						next;
						mes "";
						mes "";
						mes "FF0000Toy Factory, Level 2^000000";
						next;
						mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
						mes "If you are interested in";
						mes "a Teleport Service to these";
						mes "areas, then please vote for";
						mes "us. Would you like to vote";
						mes "for the Kafra Corporation?";
						next;
						switch(select("No","Yes")) {
						case 1:
							mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
							mes "I understand. But if you";
							mes "happen to change your mind,";
							mes "you are welcome to come back";
							mes "at any time. Thank you and";
							mes "have a good day, adventurer.";
							close2;
							cutin "kafra_09",255;
							end;
						case 2:
							set '@check,$050530_minus1_tupyo8;
							set '@check,'@check + 1;
							set lght_tupyo,'@check;
							set '@kafra,$050530_minus1_tupyo3;
							set '@kafra,'@kafra + 1;
							set $050530_minus1_tupyo3,'@kafra;
							mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
							mes "Thanks for your vote!";
							mes "We'll continue to do our best";
							mes "to provide the highest quality";
							mes "service to our customers. Have";
							mes "a good day and remember that the Kafra service is on your side~";
							close2;
							cutin "kafra_09",255;
							end;
						}
					} else if ('@kafra_point == 1) {
						mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
						mes "After totalling the number of";
						mes "votes from the last election,";
						mes "we have concluded that the";
						mes "minimum voter participation";
						mes "condition was not satisfied.";
						next;
						mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
						mes "Therefore, another election to";
						mes "determine which company will";
						mes "provide the Dungeon Teleport";
						mes "Service will be held. The Kafra";
						mes "Corporation will teleport to";
						mes "the following dungeons...";
						next;
						mes "";
						mes "";
						mes "^FF0000Toy Factory, Level 2^000000";
						mes "^FF0000Al De Baran Clock Tower, Level 3 ^000000";
						next;
						mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
						mes "If you are interested in";
						mes "a Teleport Service to these";
						mes "areas, then please vote for";
						mes "us. Would you like to vote";
						mes "for the Kafra Corporation?";
						next;
						switch(select("No","Yes")) {
						case 1:
							mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
							mes "I understand. But if you";
							mes "happen to change your mind,";
							mes "you are welcome to come back";
							mes "at any time. Thank you and";
							mes "have a good day, adventurer.";
							close2;
							cutin "kafra_09",255;
							end;
						case 2:
							set '@check,$050530_minus1_tupyo8;
							set '@check,'@check + 1;
							set lght_tupyo,'@check;

							close2;
							cutin "kafra_09",255;
							end;

	donpcevent "ScrutinyAssociation#tim5::OnCommandOn";
	end;
}

			close2;
			cutin "kafra_02",255;
			end;

	case 4:

		close2;
		cutin "kafra_02",255;
		end;
	}
}

				case 1:

						end;
					} else {
						mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
						mes "I'm sorry, but you don't";

						mes "to the Toy Factory. Please";
						mes "check your funds again.";
						close2;
						cutin "kafra_02",255;
						end;
					}
				case 2:
					if (Zeny >= 4000) {
						set Zeny,Zeny-4000;
						cutin "kafra_02",255;
						warp "alde_dun03.gat",265,22;
						end;
					} else {

					cutin "kafra_02",255;
					end;
				}
			}
		} else if ('@result == 1) {
			mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
			mes "I'm sorry, but because of";
			mes "the results from the most";
			mes "recent election, Cool Event";
			mes "Corp. is currently handling";
			mes "the Dungeon Teleport Service. We apologize for the inconvenience.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_02",255;
			end;
		} else {
			mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
			mes "I am sorry, but we do not provide Teleport Service during the vote period. You may use the service later following the result of the vote.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_02",255;
			end;
		}
	case 4:
		mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
		mes "I'm sorry, but the";
		mes "Dungeon Teleport Service";
		mes "is not active during the voting";
		mes "period. Once the election is";
		mes "over, the Dungeon Teleport";
		mes "Service will become available.";
		close2;
		cutin "kafra_02",255;
		end;
	}
}

						end;
					} else {
						mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
						mes "I'm sorry, but you don't";
						mes "have enough money to pay";
						mes "the 4,000 zeny fee to teleport";
						mes "to the Clock Tower. Please";
						mes "check your funds again.";
						close2;
						cutin "kafra_02",255;
						end;
					}
				case 3:
					if (Zeny >= 4000) {
						set Zeny,Zeny-4000;
						cutin "kafra_02",255;
						warp "mag_dun02.gat",47,40;
						end;
					} else {
						mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
						mes "I'm sorry, but you don't";
						mes "have enough money to pay";
						mes "the 4,000 zeny fee to teleport";
						mes "to the Lava Dungeon. Please";
						mes "check your funds again.";
						close2;
						cutin "kafra_02",255;
						end;
					}
				case 4:
					mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
					mes "We, here at Kafra Corporation,";
					mes "are always endeavoring to provide you with the best services. We hope that we meet your adventuring needs and standards of excellence.";
					close2;
					cutin "kafra_02",255;
					end;
				}
			}
		} else if ('@result == 1) {
			mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
			mes "I'm sorry, but because of";
			mes "the results from the most";
			mes "recent election, Cool Event";
			mes "Corp. is currently handling";
			mes "the Dungeon Teleport Service. We apologize for the inconvenience.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_02",255;
			end;
		} else {
			mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
			mes "I am sorry, but we do not provide Teleport Service during the vote period. You may use the service later following the result of the vote.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_02",255;
			end;
		}
	case 4:
		mes "[Kafra Voting Staff]";
		mes "I'm sorry, but the";
		mes "Dungeon Teleport Service";
		mes "is not active during the voting";
		mes "period. Once the election is";
		mes "over, the Dungeon Teleport";
		mes "Service will become available.";
		close2;
		cutin "kafra_02",255;
		end;
	}
}
